</div>\n      <div class="leaflet-bottom leaflet-right">\n      </div>\n     </div>\n    </div>\n   </div>\n   <div class="bottom-banner">\n    <div class="container">\n     Simple to use directive for easy embedding and interacting with a map managed with the\n     <a href="http://leafletjs.com/">\n      leaflet map library\n     </a>\n     on an\n     <a href="http://angularjs.org">\n      AngularJS\n     </a>\n     application.\n    </div>\n   </div>\n  </div>\n  <div class="container content">\n   <!-- ngView: -->\n   <ng-view class="ng-scope">\n    <div class="row ng-scope">\n     <div class="col-md-12">\n      <p>\n       This directive allows you to embed a map on your\n       <strong>\n        AngularJS\n       </strong>\n       application and interact bi-directionally with it via the\n       <a href="http://docs.angularjs.org/api/ng.$rootScope.Scope">\n        AngularJS scope\n       </a>\n       and the\n       <a href="http://leafletjs.com/reference.html">\n        leaflet map library API\n       </a>\n       . In its current state, it\'s not a full-featured library, although it\'s easy to use and extend, and a good starting point to learn to code a directive into the great AngularJS library.\n      </p>\n     </div>\n    </div>\n    <div class="row ng-scope">\n     <div class="col-md-12">\n      <p>\n       The code of the directive and this page has been inspired by the\n       <a href="http://angular-ui.github.com/angular-google-maps/">\n        Angular Google Maps\n       </a>\n       directive developed by\n       <a href="https://github.com/angular-ui/angular-google-maps">\n        nlaplante &amp; nmccready\n       </a>\n       . The initial code has been (and is being) evolved and improved by\n       <a href="https://github.com/angular-ui/ui-leaflet/graphs/contributors">\n        these contributors\n       </a>\n       .\n      </p>\n     </div>\n    </div>\n    <div class="row ng-scope">\n     <div class="col-md-12">\n      <div class="page-header">\n       <h1>\n        Getting started\n       </h1>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Before using\n       <strong>\n        angular-leaflet-directive\n       </strong>\n       , you\n        must include some javascript files to your main HTML:\n      </p>\n      <ul>\n       <li>\n        the AngularJS library,\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="https://github.com/nmccready/angular-simple-logger">\n         Angular Simple Logger\n        </a>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        the Leaflet library (javascript &amp; CSS),\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        and the ui-leaflet.js script.\n       </li>\n       <ul>\n        <li>\n         <a href="http://bower.io/search/?q=ui-leaflet">\n          Bower\n         </a>\n        </li>\n        <li>\n         <a href="https://www.npmjs.com/package/ui-leaflet">\n          npm\n         </a>\n        </li>\n        <li>\n         <a href="https://github.com/angular-ui/ui-leaflet/releases">\n          github\n         </a>\n        </li>\n       </ul>\n      </ul>\n      <br/>\n      <p>\n       Something like this:\n      </p>\n      <ul class="nav nav-tabs">\n       <li class="active">\n        <a data-toggle="tab" href="" ng-click="activeTab=\'javascript\'">\n         Javascript includes\n        </a>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a data-toggle="tab" href="" ng-click="activeTab=\'css\'">\n         CSS includes\n        </a>\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <div class="tab-container" ng-switch="" on="activeTab">\n       <!-- ngSwitchDefault: -->\n       <div class="ng-scope" hljs="" include="\'website/javascript.inc\'" ng-switch-default="">\n And that\'s all. Now you can start embedding maps to your application adding the custom tag\n      <code>\n       &lt;leaflet&gt;\n      </code>\n      with some attributes on your HTML code, and interacting with the\n      <span class="label label-danger">\n       scope\n      </span>\n      of your controller. for easy embedding and interacting with a map managed with the\n     <a href="http://leafletjs.com/">\n      leaflet map library\n     </a>\n     on an\n     <a href="http://angularjs.org">\n      AngularJS\n     </a>\n     application.\n    </div>\n   </div>\n  </div>\n  <div class="container content">\n   <!-- ngView: -->\n   <ng-view class="ng-scope">\n    <div class="row ng-scope">\n     <div class="col-md-12">\n      <p>\n       This directive allows you to embed a map on your\n       <strong>\n        AngularJS\n       </strong>\n       application and interact bi-directionally with it via the\n       <a href="http://docs.angularjs.org/api/ng.$rootScope.Scope">\n        AngularJS scope\n       </a>\n       and the\n       <a href="http://leafletjs.com/reference.html">\n        leaflet map library API\n       </a>\n       . In its current state, it\'s not a full-featured library, although it\'s easy to use and extend, and a good starting point to learn to code a directive into the great AngularJS library.\n      </p>\n     </div>\n    </div>\n    <div class="row ng-scope">\n     <div class="col-md-12">\n      <p>\n       The code of the directive and this page has been inspired by the\n       <a href="http://angular-ui.github.com/angular-google-maps/">\n        Angular Google Maps\n       </a>\n       directive developed by\n       <a href="https://github.com/angular-ui/angular-google-maps">\n        nlaplante &amp; nmccready\n       </a>\n       . The initial code has been (and is being) evolved and improved by\n       <a href="https://github.com/angular-ui/ui-leaflet/graphs/contributors">\n        these contributors\n       </a>\n       .\n      </p>\n     </div>\n    </div>\n    <div class="row ng-scope">\n     <div class="col-md-12">\n      <div class="page-header">\n       <h1>\n        Getting started\n       </h1>\n      </div>\n
